    // Achlys - Miserable Claws
    //=================================================================================================================
    "achlys_miserable_claws"
    {
        // General
        //-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        "BaseClass"                     "ability_datadriven"
        "AbilityBehavior"               "DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_UNIT_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_AUTOCAST | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_ATTACK"
        "AbilityUnitTargetTeam"         "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_ENEMY"
        "AbilityUnitTargetType"         "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_BASIC"
        "AbilityUnitTargetFlags"        "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_FLAG_MAGIC_IMMUNE_ENEMIES"
        "SpellImmunityType"             "SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_YES"
        "AbilityTextureName"            "achlys_miserable_claws"

        // Time     
        //-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        "AbilityCastRange"              "150"

        // Damage.
        //-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        "AbilityDuration"               "8"

        // Cost
        //-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        "AbilityManaCost"               "15"

        // Special
        //-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        "AbilitySpecial"
        {
            "01"
            {
                "var_type"          "FIELD_FLOAT"
                "armor_per_stack"   "-0.5 -1 -1.5 -2"
            }
            "02"
            {
                "var_type"          "FIELD_INTEGER"
                "slow_per_stack"    "-3 -4 -5 -6"
            }
            "03"
            {
                "var_type"          "FIELD_INTEGER"
                "duration"          "8"
            }
            "04"
            {
                "var_type"          "FIELD_INTEGER"
                "root_duration"     "3"
            }
        }

        // Precache
        //-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        "precache"
        {
            "soundfile" "soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_life_stealer.vsndevts"
            "soundfile" "soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_nightstalker.vsndevts"
            "particle"  "particles/econ/items/bloodseeker/bloodseeker_eztzhok_weapon/bloodseeker_bloodbath_eztzhok_burst.vpcf"
            "particle"  "particles/achlys_miserable_claws_debuff.vpcf"
            "particle"  "particles/achlys_miserable_claws_root.vpcf"
        }

        // Datadriven
        //-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        "Modifiers"
        {
            // Modifier to handle OrbEffect-Behaviour
            "modifier_achlys_miserable_claws_handler"
            {
                // Will always stay on the caster once the ability is upgraded
                // Hidden
                "Passive"           "1"
                "IsHidden"          "1"
                "IsBuff"            "0"
                "IsDebuff"          "0"
                "IsPurgable"        "0"

                // OrbEffect-Behaviour
                "Orb"
                {
                    "Priority"          "DOTA_ORB_PRIORITY_ABILITY"
                    "ProjectileName"    "particles/econ/items/bloodseeker/bloodseeker_eztzhok_weapon/bloodseeker_bloodbath_eztzhok_burst.vpcf"
                    "CastAttack"        "1"
                }

                // HealthCost is handled here
                "OnOrbFire"
                {
                    "FireSound"
                    {
                        "EffectName"    "Hero_LifeStealer.PreAttack"
                        "Target"        "CASTER"
                    }
                    "FireSound"
                    {
                        "EffectName"    "Hero_Nightstalker.Attack"
                        "Target"        "TARGET"
                    }
                    "SpendMana"
                    {
                        "Mana" "%AbilityManaCost"
                    }
                }

                // Apply the hidden dot modifier to the target here
                // Call IncreaseStackCount to keep stack count on modifier_burning_spear_datadriven_debuff_counter updated
                "OnOrbImpact"
                {
                    "ApplyModifier"
                    {
                        "ModifierName"  "modifier_achlys_miserable_claws_debuff"
                        "Target"        "TARGET"
                    }

                    "RunScript"
                    {
                        "ScriptFile"    "heroes/hero_achlys/achlys_miserable_claws"
                        "Function"      "IncreaseStackCount"
                        "modifier_counter_name"     "modifier_achlys_miserable_claws_debuff_counter"
                    }
                }
            }

            // Modifier to show stack count
            // Only visual
            "modifier_achlys_miserable_claws_debuff_counter"
            {
                "Passive"           "0"
                "IsHidden"          "0"
                "IsBuff"            "0"
                "IsDebuff"          "1"
                "IsPurgable"        "1"
                
                "OnAttacked"
                {
                    "RunScript"
                    {
                        "ScriptFile"    "heroes/hero_achlys/achlys_miserable_claws"
                        "Function"      "CheckRoot"
                    }
                }
            }

            // Modifier to handle the dot
            "modifier_achlys_miserable_claws_debuff"
            {
                "Passive"           "0"
                "IsHidden"          "1"
                "IsBuff"            "0"
                "IsDebuff"          "1"
                "IsPurgable"        "1"
                "Duration"          "%duration"
                
                "EffectName"        "particles/achlys_miserable_claws_debuff.vpcf"
                "EffectAttachType"  "follow_origin"

                // Allow multiple instances of this modifier on the target
                // Modifiers stack additivly (dmg) with independent durations
                "Attributes"        "MODIFIER_ATTRIBUTE_MULTIPLE"

                // Updating visual modifier's stack count
                "OnDestroy"
                {
                    "RunScript"
                    {
                        "ScriptFile"    "heroes/hero_achlys/achlys_miserable_claws"
                        "Function"      "DecreaseStackCount"

                        "modifier_counter_name"     "modifier_achlys_miserable_claws_debuff_counter"
                    }
                }
                "Properties"
                {
                    "MODIFIER_PROPERTY_MOVESPEED_BONUS_PERCENTAGE"  "%slow_per_stack"
                    "MODIFIER_PROPERTY_PHYSICAL_ARMOR_BONUS"        "%armor_per_stack"
                }
            }
            "modifier_achlys_miserable_claws_root"
            {
                "Passive"           "0"
                "IsHidden"          "0"
                "IsBuff"            "0"
                "IsDebuff"          "1"
                "IsPurgable"        "1"
                
                "EffectName"    "particles/achlys_miserable_claws_root.vpcf"
                "EffectAttachType"  "follow_origin"
                
                "OnCreated"
                {
                    "FireSound"
                    {
                        "EffectName"    "Hero_Bane.Nightmare"
                        "Target"        "CASTER"
                    }
                }

                "ThinkInterval" "0.03"
                "OnIntervalThink"
                {
                    "RunScript"
                    {
                        "ScriptFile"    "heroes/hero_achlys/achlys_miserable_claws"
                        "Function"      "CheckAngle"
                    }
                }
                "States"
                {
                    "MODIFIER_STATE_ROOTED" "MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
                }
            }
        }
    }

        "AbilityProcsMagicStick"        "1"

        {
            "particle"  "particles/units/heroes/hero_mirana/mirana_spell_arrow.vpcf"
            
        }
    
        "AbilitySpecial"
        {

            }
            "02"

            }
            "03"
            {
                "var_type"          "FIELD_FLOAT"
                "projectile_interval" "0.2"
            }
            "04"
            {
                "var_type"          "FIELD_INTEGER"
                "projectile_loss_dist"  "60"
            }
            "05"
            {
                "var_type"          "FIELD_INTEGER"
                "projectile_loss_dmg"   "8"
            }
            "06"
            {
                "var_type"          "FIELD_INTEGER"
                "projectile_speed"  "1200"
            }
            "07"
            {
                "var_type"          "FIELD_INTEGER"
                "duration"          "5"
            }
        }
    
        "OnSpellStart"
        {
            "RunScript"
            {
                "ScriptFile"    "heroes/eurus/feather_barrage.lua"
                "Function"      "CreateBird"
                "Target"        "POINT"
            }
    
            "ApplyModifier"
            {
                "ModifierName"  "modifier_bird_position"
                "Target"        "CASTER"
                "Duration"      "%duration"
            }
        }
    
        "OnProjectileHitUnit"
        {
            "DeleteOnHit"   "1"
            "RunScript"
            {
                "ScriptFile"    "heroes/eurus/feather_barrage.lua"
                "Function"      "ProjectileHit"
            }
        }
    
        "Modifiers"
        {   
            "modifier_bird_position"
            {
                "ThinkInterval"  "0.03"
                "OnIntervalThink"
                {
                    "RunScript"
                    {
                        "ScriptFile"    "heroes/eurus/feather_barrage.lua"
                        "Function"      "FollowHero"
                    }
                }
            }
            "modifier_feather_barrage_dummy"
            {
                "Passive"           "0"
                "IsHidden"          "0"
                "IsDebuff"          "0"
    
                "ThinkInterval"         "%projectile_interval"
                "OnIntervalThink"
                {
                    "RunScript"
                    {
                        "ScriptFile"    "heroes/eurus/feather_barrage.lua"
                        "Function"      "ShootFeathers"
                        "feather"       "particles/units/heroes/hero_mirana/mirana_spell_arrow.vpcf"
                    }
                    
                }
    
                "OnDestroy"
                {
                    "RunScript"
                    {
                        "ScriptFile"    "heroes/eurus/feather_barrage.lua"
                        "Function"      "KillBird"
                    }
                }
        
                "States"
                {
                    "MODIFIER_STATE_UNSELECTABLE"       "MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
